break-word !important;\">记者梳理政策了解到，目前全国已有28个省区市，出台了支持实体书店发展的举措。以北京市为例，在《北京市实体书店扶持资金管理办法》《北京市实体书店扶持资金项目管理实施细则》《北京市各区实体书店房租补贴标准》等政策利好下，2019年，北京市143家书店得到房租补贴，共计5300余万元，同比增加30%，极大缓解了经营者的生存压力。</span></section><p !important;\">记者：</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">实体书店复兴，扶持政策是最主要原因吗？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">政策引导是一个原因，商业吸引本身才是根本原因。政策性的补贴都是事后补，等书店开出来再补贴，因此不是前提。频繁有人进入实体书店行业或者重装扩大实体书店的规模，说到底，还是商业方面的吸引力。尤其是在热闹商圈开书店，无论租金还是装修成本，投入都不小，没人掏钱买单，肯定办不起来。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：开在核心商圈的书店，怎么才能消化前期投入成本？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这些书店不少是商业地产主动招徕入驻的，在一段时间内，场租不要钱，装修设计的钱也由他来出。书店方面只需要负担书和员工的费用，以及后续的运营成本。如果有能力的书店经营者，能够将装修成本控制住，甚至在装修过程中就可以挣钱。商业地产商看好实体书店的到来，能为他挣到更多钱。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：实体书店如何打造商业吸引力？是把书店装修成“网红”风格吗？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在网络时代之前，买书只能到书店去，因为只有那里卖书。现在购书的途径太多了，尤其网购不光方便，价格也有优势。书店的吸引力变了，成为一个文化媒介，具有传播属性。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">移动社交媒体时代，如果书店做得足够漂亮，成为“网红”打卡地，让每个来的人都想拍照发朋友圈晒图。通过这种途径，能够将书店的形象传播出去，重塑书店的吸引力。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">对于任何实体商业体来说，吸引客流都是前提基础。如果开在商圈和综合商业体当中，前来“网红”书店打卡带来的客流量，就不仅能惠及书店，还能分享给其他商家。所以商业地产才看好实体书店，愿意投入支持实体书店。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">实体书店“网红化”，也不一定是从业者主动就想让书店变成这样，而是在目前中国整个大的商业背景、消费背景，以及文化潮流的影响下，必须要呈现出的一个形态。因为在一个更大的商业循环当中，需要“网红化”的实体书店，那它就以这种“网红脸”的形象和定位站出来，满足这种新的需求。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 544px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/cuQuIn5ib4JsTj7vqBoNbC9NI9E3kDKlNhay1obabeG5kkg54ub9UVIKrC2tBu0JrgzQOHQibcRhTQZpicI1jiapYg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">7月30日中午，单向空间（朝阳大悦城店）内，咖啡座已满座，多数人在用电脑，个别人在看书。</span></section><p><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：可是被“颜值”吸引来书店打卡的多数人，似乎只拍照不买书，这是书店所期待的氛围吗？书店仍能从中受惠吗？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在这个手机占用了人们主要注意力的时代，爱读书的人在变少，这是个不争的事实。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">有些人虽然自己没买书，但是愿意到书店拍照、发朋友圈，至少表达出对读书的一种向往，说明他们内心中还是尊重书香文化的。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">即使只是为了拍照，他们的到来，让书店这种文化场所有了人气，本身也是在塑造一种崇尚阅读的文化氛围。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">通过人们到书店来拍照打卡发朋友圈，把书店的形象传播出去，把人吸引来，来的人当中总有人会看书，总有人会买书。只卖书的书店，现在也没法生存。书店也卖文创产品、咖啡和其他服务。这些都能为书店带来收入，而且毛利率都比卖书要高。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：在有的书店里，咖啡座和文创产品的占地面积远超书架。实体书店只有这样才能经营得好吗？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">经常会有人抱怨：现在的书店不像书店，更像咖啡馆、文创店，怎么能这样呢？书店从业者也很纠结：我们也想纯粹，但是一算账，为了活命，必须要做点文创，卖点咖啡轻食，搞些活动。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">我总是为书店抱屈：那些谴责书店不够纯粹的人，想必是爱书的人，但也未必会在实体书店买书，更别提只在实体书店买书。多数人还是会去网上买书。既然自诩为爱书人的你，都不一定去实体书店买书，你让实体书店怎么能只靠卖书生存呢？</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(2, 30, 170);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">政策资本双双“输血”，实体书店仍难“造血”</span></strong></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：政策对实体书店的支持，想必是看重书店的文化属性。但具备文化属性的场所很多，为什么偏对实体书店如此倾斜？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">书店作为一个文化场所，受到各级各地政府的格外重视和支持，主要是因为它惠民。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">和博物馆、美术馆、音乐厅、图书馆等其他公共文化场所相比，实体书店的建设成本更低、运营效率更高、市民覆盖面更广。像美术馆、音乐厅这样的地方，有一定的进入门槛。但是书店谁都可以进。人们逛书店不会有心理负担，担心自己看不看得懂。书店也没人会阻止你翻书，而且书比图书馆的新，很多书店都有座位，环境比多数图书馆好。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：通过政策支持实体书店，是否有违市场规律？在阅读人口下降和人均阅读数量下降的背景下，我们是否需要那么多书店？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">我觉得需要。以目前国内实体书店的数量来看，新建的计划还远达不到锦上添花的程度，而更多是在“补课”。我们还是太缺少像样的实体书店了，各地都需要这样的文化场所。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">有人会问：与其投入这么多钱支持实体书店，为什么不建更多图书馆？但是如果要运营一家图书馆，哪怕只是社区街道这个级别的，从建筑选址到人员招聘，都要经历一个较为漫长的过程，不仅投入高，效率也是个问题。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">实体书店就不一样，非常灵活，只要政策稍加引导，很容易活跃起来。政府的引导主要起到奖补作用，更主要的成本由市场承担，负担也不重。实体书店作为一个文化场所，不仅是商业主体，还能分担很多政府的公共文化职能，所以受到政策青睐。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：纵观现在的实体书店行业，有理想的商业模式和“造血”能力吗？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">应该说还没有。实体书店也不能概而论之，要分不同的类别。占比最大的新华书店，由于其体量和国资背景，转型动力没有民营书店那么强烈，当然也有很多变化。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">第二个是像西西弗、言几又、钟书阁等品牌连锁书店。他们在全国开店，店面选址主要在热门商圈中。他们用新的装潢形态和混合经营的业态，代表了实体书店行业这些年崛起的新势力。但是他们大多也仍处于探索商业模式的过程当中。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">即使个别如西西弗书店，具备一定的盈利能力，也很难说在整个行业当中，这种模式就能行得通。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">其他还有依托于集团公司的书店，诸如中信书店、建投书店；依托于高校或出版社的书店，诸如外研书店、涵芬楼书店等，承担的职能和多数实体书店不太一样，经营模式也难以复制。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">还有很多更小型更独立的民营书店，每家店都有不同的特色，绝大多数在寻找新的可能性。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(2, 30, 170);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">疫情不会给实体书店带来灭顶之灾，</span></strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(2, 30, 170);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">网购才会</span></strong></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：疫情期间，很多实体书店都在积极自救，通过直播搞线上读书会，用微信公众号推销会员卡充值，叫外卖上门送书等各种营销活动，救助效果明显吗？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">肯定有效果，但不太大。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">网络营销需要一个服务体系，从选品到陈列，从供应链到客服，都有很高的要求。在此之前，很少有实体书店有这个基础，疫情期间很难临时搭建起来。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">有些实体书店搞了店员盲选、卖会员卡等活动，虽然带来一些收入，使现金流得到一定程度的缓解，但实际上是在透支未来的营收额，相当于寅吃卯粮。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">至于直播带来的收入，就更有限了。你只能看到书店告诉你，有多少人参加他们搞的直播活动，而很少提到销售额有多少，因为太少了，不好意思说出来。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">直播不适合实体书店行业。现在直播销售都是要有价格优势才能吸引来流量，但书店是产业链的末端，定价的回旋空间很少。即使真的出现哪本书因为直播卖爆了，实体书店甚至不具备供货能力。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：疫情会拖慢实体书店的复兴节奏吗？</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">程三国：</span></strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">会有影响。例如原本想要进入这个领域的店家，可能会因此犹豫。不过疫情终究不是常态，也不会为这个行业带来灭顶之灾。真正持续威胁实体书店行业的，还是电商平台的折扣冲击。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">我们国家一直没有针对图书定价体系的法律约束。网店打折售书的力度，是实体书店永远无法做到的，也是实体书店永远的痛。哪怕很多爱书人，专门逛书店，看到了喜欢的书，也会因为价格差异，习惯性地上网购买。要想解决这个问题，恐怕只有从法律层面制定图书定价保护机制，使图书销售价格得到专门的法律保障。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">自20世纪初开始到今天，以德国、法国为代表，国外图书出版业发达的国家多先后制定了图书价格的管理机制——无论在哪里买书，价格上都不会有太大区别。也正因此，徜徉在这些国家的大街小巷上，你才会动不动就偶遇历史悠久的特色书店。如果我们国家也能有相关的制度保障，或许才能从根本上扭转实体书店目前面临的种种被动局面。    </span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">来源：“新华每日电讯”调查周刊</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">记者：尹平平</span></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><section data-style=\"text-indent: 2em;;\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">责编：杨建楠</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">校对：秦黛新</span></p></section></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-size: 16px;line-height: 25.6px;font-family: 微软雅黑;text-align: center;letter-spacing: 0.54px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"__bg_gif\" data-ratio=\"0.3818984547461369\" data-type=\"gif\" data-copyright=\"0\" data-w=\"453\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word 10:03:39","title":"自媒体乱象升级：一再造谣封不死，监管难在哪","link":"http://weixin.sogou.com/weixin?type=2&query=%E5%8D%8A%E6%9C%88%E8%B0%88+%E8%87%AA%E5%AA%92%E4%BD%93%E4%B9%B1%E8%B1%A1%E5%8D%87%E7%BA%A7%EF%BC%9A%E4%B8%80%E5%86%8D%E9%80%A0%E8%B0%A3%E5%B0%81%E4%B8%8D%E6%AD%BB%EF%BC%8C%E7%9B%91%E7%AE%A1%E9%9A%BE%E5%9C%A8%E5%93%AA","description":"<div><div><div id=\"media\" class=\"rich_media_thumb_wrp\">\n\n            <img class=\"rich_media_thumb\" src=\"http://img.100weidu.com/mmbiz_jpg/eiccNfic7OE9J7DwcxkOOkDDx7ncB41UlbUpH64AtQSDVwn3dKrV6beiaGcps8Ukb97ich1a4MqRh0Ukdic1g240kfQ?imageView2/1/w/600\">\n        </div>\n    \n\n    \n\n    <div class=\"rich_media_content\" id=\"js_content\">\n                    \n\n                    \n\n                    \n                    \n                    <section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">今年以来，特别是疫情期间，热点舆情反复上演“反转剧情”，“吃瓜”群众看得津津有味，一些传统媒体人士则自嘲：“且让新闻飞一会儿。” “反转剧情”的背后，是愈演愈烈的自媒体乱象。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">营造天朗气清的网络生态、安全可信的网络空间，是亿万网民福祉，尤其事关青少年的健康成长。半月谈记者采访发现，受经济利益驱动、平台监管不严、治理手段匮乏等影响，自媒体乱象不断，且逐步呈现运营管理机构化、内容创作组织化的特点，各种网络谣言犹如病毒，不断变异，其手段与危害都在升级。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);font-size: 28px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1</strong></span></p><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">虚实参半制造“爆点”：</span></span></span></strong></span></strong></span></strong></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">伪造嫁接、脑补细节、带节奏评论</span></span></span></strong></span></strong></span></strong></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">今年5月，一家自媒体发文说，牧民反映内蒙古自治区锡林郭勒盟西乌珠穆沁旗的草原被污染多年无人问津，同时配发令人触目惊心的航拍视频和图片。然而，环保部门实际调查结果却与自媒体反映的内容大相径庭，原来自媒体的视频是经过特殊处理的。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“这是当前一种典型的造谣方式。”江苏省公安厅网安总队监控支队有关负责人说，从造谣的内容来看，以往的谣言大都是一段文字，现在升级了，不仅有文字，还有图片、视频来“佐证”。不过这些图片、视频大都是嫁接或伪造的。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"1.01875\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/eiccNfic7OE9J7DwcxkOOkDDx7ncB41UlbqgTjuHz4ee54NWexy2ndKBMhL6g2WvU6ju5cxXa6WI9YYl8WllTwaw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">这位负责人还告诉半月谈记者，今年早些时候，在新冠肺炎疫情初起时，有网民发帖称，3具尸体躺在武汉红十字会医院内一上午无人问津，也配发了现场视频。然而，调查证实，视频是很早以前的视频，反映的事件与疫情毫无关联，捏造者对视频进行了重新配音。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“脑补”是当前网络谣言的另一个惯用伎俩。江苏省公安厅网安总队有关负责人介绍，这类网络谣言多以热点新闻事实为文章主干，然后杜撰各种细节进行渲染，文章虚实参半，比之以往的纯粹捏造，让人更加难辨真假。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">今年2月，原南京医学院“3·24”强奸杀人案告破引起关注。案件告破第二天，南京公安尚未披露破案详情时，一篇“脑补”式“报道”却率先在朋友圈、微信群流传开来，点击量迅速突破10万+。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“报道”详细披露了案件侦破经过，称受害者的师兄通过关系搞到遗留在受害者体内的嫌疑人精液DNA样本，分发给群里的各位学长学妹，然后借疫情检测之机各种比对，最终比对上嫌疑人舅舅，继而又通过Y染色体找到嫌疑人。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“报道”有鼻子有眼，各种细节让人不由得不信。可是，经南京公安核实，这是一篇地地道道的虚假报道。文中嫌疑人姓氏、年龄都对，破案也的确是依赖Y染色体基因图谱技术，但其他破案细节都是杜撰的，既不是受害人师兄的功劳，也不是从舅舅找到嫌疑人，而是南京公安28年盯案不放、不破不休的结果。事后，南京警方召集媒体紧急辟谣，可仍有不少民众半信半疑，甚至说警方在抢功。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“带节奏”的评论，也是一种升级的造谣方式。这类网评紧跟热点，听起来义正辞严，然而其引用的事实、数据并不真实，而是根据制造噱头的需要，故意歪曲事实，将读者观点带偏。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">最近发生在南京的“寒门大学生偷外卖”的反转舆情，就是这样一个典型案例。最初，警方通过多家媒体发布信息，交代了当事人是某公司职员，说明了偷外卖是因为自己的外卖被偷，起了报复之心。然而，一些自媒体的评论，抓住“考研大学生”“家中其他3姐妹辍学”的细节大做文章，最终演绎成“寒门大学生因饥饿偷外卖被刑拘”，将一个普通刑案硬生生推上热搜。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);font-size: 28px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2</strong></span></p><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">管不了，也管不好？</span></span></span></strong></span></strong></span></strong></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">经济与政治交织危害大</span></span></span></strong></span></strong></span></strong></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“管不了，也管不好。”江苏苏南地区一位网信办负责人说，基层网信办对自媒体几乎没什么管理手段，遇不实报道，很难属地管理，大都需要层层上报请求上级处理，上报和反馈的速度远远赶不上谣言传播速度。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“道高一尺魔高一丈。”一些基层网信办负责人还告诉半月谈记者，为应对网信部门监管，同时更多获取网民点击、转发，一些不良自媒体在手段、技术上也不断翻新，让网信部门疲于应付。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">最典型的是“转世号”，一再造谣却封不了。江苏省公安厅网安总队有关负责人告诉半月谈记者，一个名为“微客铁汁5”的账号曾多次在网上造谣，被相关平台查封多次，但每次查封后，更改一下账户名最后的数字，就又“复活”了。疫情期间，这一账号因造谣再次被查封，已转了“5世”。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">更胆大的是，还有自媒体为了让谣言更可信，竟冒充警方账号。不久前，江苏省无锡市公安局破获一起网络水军案，相关涉案团伙控制的公众号达200多个。这一团伙将其中一个公众号伪装成警方的账号，取名“警花说事”，头像也换成一个穿着制服的女警，让很多网民，包括网信部门，误以为这就是一个警方的公众号。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">江苏省网信办有关处室负责人告诉半月谈记者，最近出现一种新的自媒体造谣方式，一些内容与标题严重不符的恶意“标题党”链接在微信群、朋友圈频频出现。调查发现，此类不良信息竟是通过锁定IP地址、GPS、手机号码等方式确定位置信息，动态转变标题，诱导读者点击，通过“蜘蛛池”等引流技术跳转至各类非法暗链地址，最终达到非法获利的目的，严重扰乱属地网络传播秩序。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“针对传统的网络谣言，许多网民已经有了一定抵抗力，然而这些变异的网络谣言更具迷惑性。”江苏省公安厅网安总队相关负责人说，特别是一些不良自媒体、网络大V逐利“粉丝经济”，将大量境外谣言“倒灌”至国内，将商业利益与政治目的交织在一起，严重危害社会稳定。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">内蒙古自治区一位基层网信办负责人认为，一些不良自媒体在制造舆论热点，获取流量与收益的同时，不惜歪曲历史与事实，传播错误价值导向，激发网络负面情绪，甚至散播民粹主义，对网络环境及社会稳定产生较大负面影响，降低了传统媒体、政府的公信力，还在不断辟谣中浪费大量行政资源。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">这位负责人还介绍，通过大量案例调查发现，自媒体逐步呈现出运营管理机构化、内容创作组织化的特点。尤其一些靠曝光吸引关注度的自媒体，从内容制作到推送都是团队化运营，以更大程度吸引流量，实现价值转化。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);font-size: 28px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">3</strong></span></p><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">话语权给了个人，监管模式也应变革</span></span></span></strong></span></strong></span></strong></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“反转新闻”何时休？自媒体究竟该怎么管？一些研究学者认为，相关监管部门应当认清自媒体属性，再推行有针对性的举措。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">南京大学新闻传播学院副院长胡翼青说，虚假报道、网络谣言是世界性难题，并非中国所独有，它与自媒体几乎是相伴相生的。这些自媒体制造网络谣言，有的不一定是要读者相信它的报道或言论，而是要你点开链接，点击其广告。自媒体造谣制造热点，与其盈利模式密切相关。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">一些专家还指出，传统媒体机构对其从业人员一般都要进行专业培训，发稿前都有相应的把关流程，追逐舆论热点的同时，坚持新闻的真实性、准确性。自媒体则不同，它搭建在一些社交网络平台之上，将话语权给了个人，而每个人的文化层次、道德观念、个人利益诉求都不一样，又缺乏专业培训，规则和底线意识不足，各种谣言自然层出不穷。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">今年疫情期间，清华大学教授沈阳就新冠肺炎疫情期间，中美两国间的谣言进行了建构分析。他认为，要管好自媒体，遏制谣言，必须了解其特性，有针对性地采取措施。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.70625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/eiccNfic7OE9J7DwcxkOOkDDx7ncB41UlbukCOULiaabInfjDSia22rthLSBhxXp4yOGfAQDib7Y9vwlq6tY6NTBfTQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">一些业内人士和基层网信部门人员建言，<strong>首先，应当强化自媒体服务平台的主体监督责任，增加其失职监督的责任成本。</strong>当前舆论环境已经发生改变，人们大多通过一些社交网络平台获取信息，这些平台应对信息发布加强把关，增加责任意识，避免一些不良账号不断死而复生。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">二是强化网络自治。</span></strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">一些专家认为，依靠相关部门有限的力量，监管面广量大的自媒体，是管不住的，必须转变监管模式和思路，强化网络自治，一方面提升群众对谣言的“抵抗力”，另一方面畅通不良信息举报渠道。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">三是要对广告联盟进行治理。</span></strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">一些基层网信办工作人员认为，自媒体制造谣言，目的在于获取流量，进而获得广告分成。需要推动广告联盟的治理，从根上遏制网络谣言。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">四是进一步加大对造谣信息发布主体的处罚力度，尽快建立失信黑名单制度。</span></strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><strong><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></strong></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">另外，还有一些业内人员建言，传统媒体要增强舆论监督报道、深度调查报道能力，抢占网络空间，对冲自媒体虚假报道带来的影响，提升舆论引导力。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">来源：《半月谈》2020年第16期<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">半月</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">谈记者：朱国亮 张丽娜 | 编辑：<span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">原碧霞</span></span></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><section data-style=\"text-indent: 2em;;\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">责编：杨建楠</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">校对：秦黛新</span></p></section></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-size: 16px;line-height: 25.6px;font-family: 微软雅黑;text-align: center;letter-spacing: 0.54px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><img class=\"__bg_gif\" data-ratio=\"0.3818984547461369\" data-type=\"gif\" data-copyright=\"0\" data-w=\"453\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">问题2：</span></strong></span></section><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif justify rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">管壁薄强度差  转椅五星脚会断裂</span></strong><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">有些办公椅在检测过程中底座出现了断裂。据检测人员介绍，五星脚是转椅重要的零部件，起着承载人体重量的作用。如果为了节约成本，金属五星脚把管壁做薄一点，或者使用了强度较差的五星脚，日常使用时发生断裂，就可能造成使用者摔伤。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages __bg_gif\" data-ratio=\"0.5515625\" border-box break-word><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">此次抽查对办公椅的底座静载荷也进行了检测。在实验室，检测人员对五星脚施加压力，刚一接触，五星脚就裂开了。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">经过检测结果发现，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">安吉上墅谢氏家具厂生产的老板椅和安吉优格家具有限公司生产的电竞椅底座静载荷不合格，可能存在致人摔伤的风险。</strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">办公椅甲醛超标 严重会致癌</span></strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">安吉递铺日昇家具厂、辽宁康富家具制造有限公司和上海恩荣办公家具有限公司各有一批次办公椅被检出甲醛释放量不合格。</strong>据介绍，长期在甲醛释放量超标的环境中，对人体的呼吸道会有一定的影响，甚至会致癌。</span></section><section break-word !important;\">上海优典家具有限公司、广州市百利文仪实业有限公司等11家企业的11批次办公椅都被检出阻燃性不合格，这些全都是公共场所用办公椅。</strong></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, 1px;\">公共场所往往是人口集中、建筑复杂的地方，如果办公椅阻燃性能不合格，火灾发生时，不但起不到阻止火势蔓延的作用，相反还会助长火焰燃烧，可能造成严重的人员伤亡事故。</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, 10:03:39","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 10:03:39","title":"泰安：这样大安","link":"http://weixin.sogou.com/weixin?type=2&query=%E5%8D%8A%E6%9C%88%E8%B0%88+%E6%B3%B0%E5%AE%89%EF%BC%9A%E8%BF%99%E6%A0%B7%E5%A4%A7%E5%AE%89","description":"<div><div><div id=\"media\" class=\"rich_media_thumb_wrp\">\n\n            <img class=\"rich_media_thumb\" class=\"rich_media_content\" id=\"js_content\">\n                    \n\n                    \n\n                    \n                    \n                    <section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“峨峨东岳高，秀极冲青天。” 因世界自然和文化双遗产泰山而名扬天下的山东省泰安市，名字里蕴含着“国泰民安”的美好寓意。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">坐拥世界级名山，泰安算好文化、生态、民生“三本账”，实现山更绿、水更清、天更蓝、城更美、人民更幸福。如今的泰安不仅是文化旅游之城、生态宜居之城，更是一座幸福魅力之城。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);font-size: 28px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1</strong></span></p><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">守护地方文化，方成泰山之大</span></span></span></strong></span></strong></span></strong></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“来者何人，俺乃泰山石敢当！”在巍峨的泰山脚下，有600多年历史的泰山皮影戏与泰山文化相得益彰。民间素有“登泰山不看泰山皮影戏不成游也”“不看影戏不知礼义”的谚语。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">泰山皮影以其雕刻精美的艺术造型、奇妙精湛的演出技巧、委婉优美的音乐唱腔在众多的皮影流派中独树一帜，享有“泰山文化活化石”的美誉。2011年泰山皮影被联合国教科文组织列入“世界级非物质文化遗产”。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">作为五岳之首，泰山留下了众多文化遗存，如今拥有联合国人类非物质文化遗产1个、国家级非物质文化遗产11个、省级非物质文化遗产42个。泰安对非遗实施创造性保护开发，使其焕发出新的生命力。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">泰山糖画、大汶口花边技艺、宁阳福葫芦制作技艺……今年6月，50余项传统医药、传统技艺、传统民俗类优秀非遗项目汇聚泰安肥城，以“线上直播+线下互动”形式邀市民共享文化盛宴，受到热捧。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“像这样的非遗展演活动，不乏国家级非遗展演项目，游客可以现场看展演、品美食、做剪纸、刻铜炉、听戏曲、买面塑，游客可以面对面、近距离领略非遗文化魅力。”泰安市文旅局局长苏雪峰说。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.66640625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/eiccNfic7OE9J7DwcxkOOkDDx7ncB41Ulb9wsgxP9g0FBlhLpsJDOSCNy7vZSHyG6h5IhsONeMwFK2EPYibMZmNAA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">游客在泰山西神门游览 郭绪雷 摄</span><br></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">泰山是道教文化的重要发源地之一，位于泰山极顶的碧霞祠至今已有1000多年的历史。山东省道教协会会长、泰山碧霞祠管委会主任张诚达说，为抵御商业化的不正之风，如今的碧霞祠坚决杜绝抽签、算命、看相等乱象，同时向游客信众免费提供环保香，并取消强制门票，实行自愿购票制度。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">泰安还依托乡土文化，打造一批“望得见山、看得见水、留得住乡愁”的特色乡村旅游产品。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">在泰山西麓北张村， 一幅幅巨幅墙绘让曾经灰白一片的村庄变成了汇集潮流与艺术的“网红地”。村子还利用闲置院落，建设精品民宿、咖啡屋等休闲娱乐设施，打出了“花田北张”旅游品牌。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">在泰山九女峰片区，像北张村这样的特色村庄一共有19个，它们如珍珠般散落在群山之中，一条25公里的环山路将它们串珠成链，形成旅游观光带。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.66640625\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/eiccNfic7OE9J7DwcxkOOkDDx7ncB41UlbZXSLFF8W4qLGrgCJ8aibTPiaf4dMFHRSKkb8iay8cwhCA8QA4saficnRjw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">初夏的泰山碧霞祠 郭绪雷 摄</span></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);font-size: 28px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2</strong></span></p><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">生态修复让古泰山焕发新生机</span></span></span></strong></span></strong></span></strong></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">森林覆盖率95.8%、植被覆盖率达97％，野生鸟类已由2002年的155种增加到2020年的338种……得益于泰山生态环境条件不断改善，如今的泰山已成为巨大的生态屏障和重要的种质资源库。建成的“泰山古树健康监测系统”，为1.8万株古树名木建立起“电子身份证”，系统记录着古树的长势、地理位置、受损程度等重要信息，管理人员可根据系统测算出古树状态是健康、衰弱，还是濒死。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">在泰安市徂汶景区湿地公园，水鸟咸集，芦苇丛生，汶河水岸坡面上皆是绿植，绿化区域内的几个节点广场三季有花、四季常绿。“夏天，这里的气温比周边平均低两三度，许多人都过来乘凉。”在公园纳凉的市民李志杰说。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">2017年底，泰山区域山水林田湖草生态保护修复工程被纳入国家试点项目，大汶河片区是泰安市重点进行保护修复的区域之一。经过改造，昔日以脏乱差闻名的泮河，蜕变为4A级景区标准的城市中央公园。河道两岸建起了回迁楼，社区儿童上学好像走在花园中。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">如今的徂汶景区，温泉、生态湿地、广阔沙滩地、白鹭栖息地遍布河岸，仅汶河国家湿地公园就拥有水生植物10余种200余万株，栖息鸟类100余种上万只，再现了诗人姚鼐所描绘的“望晚日照城郭，汶水徂徕如画”的山水胜景。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">泰安市委书记崔洪刚说，全方位、全地域、全过程的生态保护修复，改变了过去“头痛医头、脚痛医脚”的治理模式，让古老泰山焕发出蓬勃生机。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);font-size: 28px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">3</strong></span></p><hr style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center rgb border-box break-word><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center border-box break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 20px;color: rgb(51, 102, 153);letter-spacing: 1px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“绝不把历史遗留问题再留给历史”</span></span></span></strong></span></strong></span></strong></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></p><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">建成于2008年的泰安宝龙国际社区，由于部分业主违章建筑侵占规划绿地面积，导致竣工验收手续无法办理，没有违建的业主跟着受连累，500多名业主无法办理房产证，居民在子女上学、办理工商登记、落户等诸多方面遇到不便。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">在泰安市区，像宝龙国际社区这样的问题小区有上百个，涉及7.5万多个家庭。“绝不能把历史遗留问题再留给历史。要从群众最急最忧最盼的问题入手，以实际行动当好新时代泰山‘挑山工’。”崔洪刚说。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">2019年7月9日，针对部分群众反映强烈的购房后不能办证的问题，泰安成立了由市长任组长的“7·9”工作专班，集中开展房地产开发历史遗留问题专项整治。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">按照以往流程和政策，像宝龙国际这样的社区，只要有一户违建还在，规划中的绿地率就达不到，开发商就拿不到产权总证，业主也就办不了“小证”。工作专班创新受理流程，将登记与违章处置分离，先给开发商和没有违建的业主办证。与此同时，违建只要拆除完毕并恢复成绿地，相关业主也可以办证。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“房子住了10多年，以前没有不动产证，光为孙子就近入学就费了不少心，开过很多次居住证明。现在拿到证了，心里踏实了，小区的环境也提升了一个档次。”王兴霞已经入住宝龙国际社区达10年，今年3月终于拿到了不动产证，她“心中的房子”终于落地了。　</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">目前，泰安已累计整治333个、816万平方米的问题项目，为7.5万户家庭办证扫清了障碍，惠及20多万群众。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">解决房地产遗留问题，仅仅是泰安算好“民生账”的一个缩影。为缓解节假日来泰安旅游车辆堵塞道路和停放不便的问题，泰安主动将市政中心停车场让给游客，外地车辆可以在国家法定节假日免费停放。泰安还将位于城区核心位置、占地192亩估值近10亿元的土地建成当地最大的健身公园——生态绿地健身活动公园，让泰安市民可以尽情挥洒汗水、享受快乐。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1px;\">“惠及民生舍得投入，我们‘赚’来的是生态环境的持续改善和城市的可持续发展，‘赚’来的是百姓对城市发展的参与度和获得感。”崔洪刚说。</span></section><section style=\"line-height: 2em;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, !important;\"></span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box
